	desc = NW_JAP_looser.0.d
	picture = GFX_NW_JAP_looser.0
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP_looser.0" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_looser.0.a
		add_stability = 0.15
	}
}

}

# Массовые митинги на улицах
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP_looser.8
	title = NW_JAP_looser.8.t
	desc = NW_JAP_looser.8.d
	picture = GFX_NW_JAP_looser.8
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = THE_MOTHER_OF_ORDER_FLAG
			has_global_flag = WORLD_OF_SPLIT_FLAG
		}
		has_idea = JAP_growth_of_party_combat_organizations_idea
		has_stability < 0.15
		fascism > 0.25
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP_looser.8" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_looser.8.a
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP_looser.9 days = 1 } }
	}
}

# Ошибочное предсказание
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP_looser.11
	title = NW_JAP_looser.11.t
	desc = NW_JAP_looser.11.d
	picture = GFX_NW_JAP_looser.11
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP_looser.11" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_looser.11.a
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_war_support = -0.25
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.05 }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				OR = {
					capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe }
					original_tag = USA
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_embrace_pacifism_op
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

# Японцы предлагают перемирие
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP_looser.12
	title = NW_JAP_looser.12.t
	desc = NW_JAP_looser.12.d
	picture = GFX_NW_JAP_looser.12
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP_looser.12" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_looser.12.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				enemies_strength_ratio > 2
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -6
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -4
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP_looser.13 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_looser.12.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		FROM = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				white_peace = { tag = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ENG }
			every_state = {
				limit = { OR = { state = 333 state = 336 state = 1174 state = 1183 state = 1184 } }
				if = {
					limit = { controller = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
					transfer_state_to = FROM
				}
			}
			BRM = {
				if = {
					limit = { exists = yes is_subject_of = ROOT }
					ROOT = { end_puppet = PREV }
				}
				FROM = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
						set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_subject }
						else = { puppet = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = event_target:NW_france_scope }
			every_state = {
				limit = { OR = { state = 671 state = 670 state = 286 state = 741 state = 1179 state = 1180 state = 1181 state = 728 } }
				if = {
					limit = { controller = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
					transfer_state_to = FROM
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { OR = { state = 672 state = 334 state = 335 state = 667 state = 673 state = 668 state = 669 state = 738 state = 1163 } }
				if = {
					limit = { controller = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
					transfer_state_to = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.4
	title = NW_JAP.4.t
	desc = NW_JAP.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.208
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = JAP_Hirota_Koki_office
			has_completed_focus = JAP_new_Okada_government
		}
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.4" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.4.a
		add_ideas = JAP_movement_for_One_Party
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.5 days = 30 }
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.26 days = 360 }
		}
		
		if = { 
			limit = { has_power_balance = { id = JAP_new_Okada_government_power_balance } }
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = JAP_new_Okada_government_power_balance
				value = 0.05
				tooltip_side = JAP_opponents_of_democracy
			}
		}
	}
}

# Создание Тохокай
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.7
	title = NW_JAP.7.t
	desc = NW_JAP.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_7
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { NOT = { has_government = monarchy } }
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.7" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.7.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.02 }
		set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = JAP_fascism_party1_long name = JAP_fascism_party1 }
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Seigo_Nakano
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = totalism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { JAP_supporter_of_parliamentary_politics JAP_charismatic_agitator }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.317 days = 60 } }
	}
}

# Новый Токио
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.8
	title = NW_JAP.8.t
	desc = NW_JAP.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.8
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.8" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.8.a
		add_ideas = JAP_construction_of_the_new_tokyo_idea
		custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_new_capital_tt
		hidden_effect = { set_province_name = { id = 7157 name = JAP_new_capital } }
		set_capital = { state = 532 }
		532 = {
			add_victory_points = {
				province = 7157
				value = 30
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = supply_node
				province = 7157
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = fuel_silo
						size > 4
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.8.b
	}
}

# Результаты новых выборов
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.9
	title = NW_JAP.9.t
	desc = NW_JAP.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_9
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.9" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.9.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.357 days = 100 }
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.387 days = 1512 }
		}
		#effect_tooltip = { unlock_national_focus = JAP_Machid_Chunji_office }
		custom_effect_tooltip = NW_JAP_9_tt
		#set_country_flag = JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_UNLOCK_flag
		set_country_flag = JAP_skip_election_of_1940
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = monarchy popularity = -0.03 }
		set_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag
		
		set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic }
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Machida_Chuji
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = social_liberalism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { JAP_a_staunch_commoner JAP_progressive }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			meta_effect = { 
				text = { 
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = var:current_party_ideology_group
						elections_allowed = yes
						last_election = [DATE]
					}
				}
				DATE = "[GetDate]"
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = social_liberalism 
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.29
	title = NW_JAP.29.t
	desc = NW_JAP.29.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_29
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.29" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.29.a
		create_dynamic_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			add_political_power = 100
			ROOT = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					limit = { OR = { is_core_of = HCP is_core_of = EHB is_core_of = SHX } }
					transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
					set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_subject }
					else = { puppet = PREV }
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_the_Great_Han_State
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 1	}
				set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = CSR_neutrality_party3 name = CSR_neutrality_party3 }
			hidden_effect = { CSR = { CSR_wang_ying = { set_nationality = PREV.PREV } } }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = CSR_wang_ying
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = despotism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = {  }
				}
			}
#			load_focus_tree = 
#			complete_national_focus = 
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.28.b
		create_dynamic_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			add_political_power = 100
			ROOT = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					limit = { OR = { is_core_of = HCP is_core_of = EHB is_core_of = SHX } }

					else = { puppet = PREV }
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_the_Great_Han_State
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 1	}
				set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = CSR_neutrality_party3 name = CSR_neutrality_party3 }
			hidden_effect = { CSR = { CSR_wang_ying = { set_nationality = PREV.PREV } } }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = CSR_wang_ying
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = despotism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = {  }
				}
			}
#			load_focus_tree = 
#			complete_national_focus = 
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}

					character = HCP_van_kemin

				}
			}

					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {

						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {

					character = HCP_van_kemin
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = liberalism
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}

	option = {

					else = { puppet = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = HCP_van_kemin
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {

		trigger = { original_tag = JAP }
	}
	title = {
		text = NW_JAP.35.t.b
		trigger = { original_tag = SOV }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.35.d.a
		trigger = { original_tag = JAP }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.35.d.b
		trigger = { original_tag = SOV }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_35
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		JAP = {
			check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 10 }
			all_enemy_country = { is_major = no }
			controls_state = 527
		}
		SOV = { 
			controls_state = 984
			all_enemy_country = { is_major = no }
			has_civil_war = no
		}
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.35" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.35.a
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = JAP }
			activate_mission = JAP_preparing_for_Chankufen
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.647 days = 5 } 
			SOV = { activate_mission = JAP_preparing_for_Chankufen }
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				activate_mission = JAP_preparing_for_Chankufen
				JAP = { activate_mission = JAP_preparing_for_Chankufen }
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = NW_JAP.47.a

			modifier = {
				add = -1
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { is_literally_china = yes }
			white_peace = { tag = ROOT }
		}
		FROM = { annex_country = { target = HCP transfer_troops = yes } }
		1031 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		1145 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		608 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		1132 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }

			limit = { country_exists = MEN }
			MEN = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.48 hours = 6 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CSR }
			CSR = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.48 hours = 6 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.0 days = 1 } }
	}

			controls_state = 1145
			controls_state = 1031
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }

	}

		name = NW_JAP.77.a

			limit = { has_idea = JAP_Seva }
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.76 hours = 6 }

				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_restavration_Seva_Reiva } } complete_national_focus = JAP_restavration_Seva_Reiva }
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_increase_the_participation_of_the_Emperor_in_political_life } } complete_national_focus = JAP_increase_the_participation_of_the_Emperor_in_political_life }
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_imperial_support_for_reforms } } complete_national_focus = JAP_imperial_support_for_reforms }
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_invite_Ikki_Kita } } complete_national_focus = JAP_invite_Ikki_Kita }
			}
		}
	}

		trigger = { has_idea = JAP_Reiva }
	}

	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.102.a
		USA = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.105 days = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = enemies
					has_country_flag = china_declare_government_flag
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china = yes
					has_country_flag = china_declare_government_flag
					is_faction_leader = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.106 days = 4 random_days = 3 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { is_literally_china = yes is_faction_leader = yes has_war_with = ROOT }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.106 days = 4 random_days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.102.b
		USA = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.103 days = 1 } }
	}
}

			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				enemies_strength_ratio > 2
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -6
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -4
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.8 days = 1 } }
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_embargoing = FROM }
				break_embargo = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				white_peace = { tag = PREV }
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } NOT = { original_tag = MAN } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.106.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		USA = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.107 days = 1 } }

		country_exists = FIC
		NOT = {
			has_subject = FIC
			has_active_mission = JAP_discontent_of_the_military_mission
		}
		check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 15 }
		JAP_Yosuke_Matsuoka = {
			is_political_advisor = no
			NOT = { is_character_slot = political_advisor }
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.118" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.118.a
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.9 days = 1 }
			USA = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.119 days = 1 } }
		}
		set_country_flag = JAP_break_ties_with_the_French_in_Indochina_UNLOCK_flag
		unlock_decision_tooltip = JAP_break_ties_with_the_French_in_Indochina
		FIC = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_subject = yes }
				OVERLORD = { end_puppet = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
				ROOT = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
			add_ideas = JAP_japanese_occupation
		}
	}

# JAP Американское эмбарго
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.121
	title = NW_JAP.121.t
	desc = NW_JAP.121.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_121
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.121" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.121.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hideki_Todze ruling_only = yes } } }
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Hideki_Todze
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_representative_of_Toseikha }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_Todze_office } }
			complete_national_focus = JAP_Todze_office
		}
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = JAP_operation_Z_category
		activate_mission = JAP_tora_tora_tora
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.121.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.123 days = 1 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 20 } }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.137 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# JAP Предварительные условия
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.128
	title = NW_JAP.128.t
	desc = NW_JAP.128.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_128
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.128" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.128.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var < 10 } }
		FIC = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = JAP_japanese_occupation }
				remove_ideas = JAP_japanese_occupation
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_military_access_to = ROOT }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				ROOT = { end_puppet = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			event_target:NW_france_scope = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
					end_wars = no
					end_civil_wars = no
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.129 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.128.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.135 days = 1 } }
	}
}

				limit = { is_embargoing = FROM }
				break_embargo = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				white_peace = { tag = PREV }
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } NOT = { original_tag = MAN } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = JAP_the_Great_Peacemaker
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.132 days = 20 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.131.b
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.11 days = 1 } }
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_embargoing = FROM }
				break_embargo = FROM
			}
		}

				limit = { has_idea = JAP_japanese_occupation }
				remove_ideas = JAP_japanese_occupation
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_military_access_to = FROM }

					country = FROM
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}

				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV

					end_wars = no
					end_civil_wars = no
				}
			}
			add_ideas = JAP_Asian_Switzerland_idea
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.133
	title = NW_JAP.133.t
	desc = NW_JAP.133.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_133
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.133" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.133.a
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.12 days = 1 } }
		kill_country_leader = yes
		retire_character = JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = -15 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = fascism }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = JAP_Yosuke_Matsuoka
					JAP_Yosuke_Matsuoka = {
						is_country_leader = no
						NOT = { has_character_flag = JAP_Yosuke_Matsuoka_sick }
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Yosuke_Matsuoka
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nationalism_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_former_President_of_Mantetsu JAP_master_of_a_Hundred_Thousand_Words }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_Matsuoka_Office } }
					complete_national_focus = JAP_Matsuoka_Office
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Seigo_Nakano
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = totalism
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_supporter_of_parliamentary_politics JAP_charismatic_agitator }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = neutrality }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Prince_Naruhito ruling_only = yes } } }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Prince_Naruhito
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_bad_reputation_in_the_imperial_house JAP_liberal_imperialist JAP_a_mad_political_schemer }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_Naruhiko_office } }
				complete_national_focus = JAP_Naruhiko_office
			}
		}
	}
}

# JAP Начало переговоров с монгольской делегацией
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.160
	title = NW_JAP.160.t
	desc = NW_JAP.160.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_145_160
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.160" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.160.a
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.15 days = 35 } }
		FROM = {
			#MON и JAP
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = ROOT
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
		MAN = {
			#MON и MAN
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = FROM
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = FROM
			}
			#SOV и MAN
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = SOV
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = SOV
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			#SOV и клики
			limit = { is_literally_china = yes NOT = { original_tag = MON original_tag = MAN is_subject_of = ROOT is_subject_of = SOV } }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_2_op
				target = SOV
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_2_op
				target = SOV
			}
			#JAP и клики
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_2_op
				target = ROOT
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_2_op
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.174.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_war = no
				FROM = { has_war = yes }
			}
		}
		diplomatic_relation = { country = FROM relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.174.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 65 }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 35 }
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 5 }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value < 35 }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value < 65 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_war = yes
				FROM = { has_war = no }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Обсуждение бюджета на предстоящий год
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.175
	title = NW_JAP.175.t
	desc = NW_JAP.175.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_190_193
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_law_on_national_mobilization_flag }
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.175" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.175.a
		add_political_power = -20
		if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 10 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
			JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.175 days = 365 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.175.b
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.176 days = 365 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.175.c
		add_stability = -0.1 
		add_ideas = JAP_increase_of_inflation_idea 
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes		
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.177 days = 365 } }
	}
}

# Напряжённое обсуждение бюджета
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.176
	title = NW_JAP.176.t
	desc = NW_JAP.176.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_190_193
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_law_on_national_mobilization_flag }
		has_government = neutrality
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.176" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.175.a
		add_political_power = -20
		if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 10 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
			JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.175 days = 365 } }
		if = { 
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_increase_of_inflation_idea }
			remove_ideas = JAP_increase_of_inflation_idea 
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.175.b
		add_political_power = -50
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = JAP_increase_of_inflation_idea } }
			add_ideas = JAP_increase_of_inflation_idea 
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.177 days = 365 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.175.c
		add_stability = -0.1 
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes		
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.178 days = 10 } }
	}
}

# Экономический кризис
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.178
	title = NW_JAP.178.t
	desc = { 
		text = NW_JAP.178.d.a
		trigger = { 
			OR = { 
				has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hirota_Koki ruling_only = yes }
				AND = { 
					NOT = { 
						has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hirota_Koki ruling_only = yes }
						has_country_flag = JAP_Lord_Konoe
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { 
		text = NW_JAP.178.d.b
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hirota_Koki ruling_only = yes } }
	}
	desc = { 
		text = NW_JAP.178.d.c
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { 
				has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hirota_Koki ruling_only = yes }
				has_country_flag = JAP_Lord_Konoe
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_190_193
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_law_on_national_mobilization_flag }
		has_government = neutrality
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.178" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.178.a
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hirota_Koki ruling_only = yes } } 
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Shigeru_Yoshida_bureaucrat
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { JAP_representative_of_reform_bureaucrats }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = JAP_Fumio_Goto_office_UNLOCK_flag
		set_country_flag = JAP_Hirota_Koki_has_resigned_flag
		complete_national_focus = JAP_discussion_of_the_new_budget_plan
		effect_tooltip = { unlock_national_focus = JAP_Fumio_Goto_office }		
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.178.b
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { 
				has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hirota_Koki ruling_only = yes }
				has_country_flag = JAP_Lord_Konoe
			} 
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_Fumimaro_Konoe } }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Fumimaro_Konoe
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = "POLITICS_FUMIMARO_KONOE_DESC"
					ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { JAP_ambitious_political_views JAP_the_melancholic_Prince2 JAP_opponent_of_the_war_with_the_United_States }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { promote_character = JAP_Fumimaro_Konoe }
		set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party8 name = JAP_neutrality_party8 }
		activate_mission = JAP_time_to_retirement
		activate_mission = JAP_change_of_mood
	#	hidden_effect = { 
	#		country_event = NW_JAP.740
	#		country_event = NW_JAP.742
	#		country_event = NW_JAP.744
	#	}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.178.c
		OR = { 
			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hirota_Koki ruling_only = yes }
			AND = { 
				NOT = { 
					has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hirota_Koki ruling_only = yes }
					has_country_flag = JAP_Lord_Konoe
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = NW_JAP.723
	}
}

			#	complete_national_focus = JAP_Matsuoka_Office
			#}
		}
		else = { 
			if = {
				limit = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_Hiranuma_Kiichiro }
				promote_character = JAP_Hiranuma_Kiichiro
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Hiranuma_Kiichiro
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						desc = "POLITICS_HIRANUMA_KIICHIRO_DESC"
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_the_hidden_schemer JAP_a_representative_of_the_old_elites }
					}
				}
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party10 name = JAP_neutrality_party10 }
		}
	}
}

	desc = NW_JAP.231.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_231
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.231" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.231.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				enemies_strength_ratio > 2
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -6
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -4
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { OR = { original_tag = FROM is_in_faction_with = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } }
			white_peace = { tag = ROOT }
		}
		annex_country = { target = HCP transfer_troops = yes }
		1031 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		1145 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		608 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		1132 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = MEN }
			MEN = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.48 hours = 6 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CSR }
			CSR = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.48 hours = 6 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.30 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.231.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.232 days = 1 } }
	}
}

					set_politics = {

					}

		}

	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.236.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity } }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity = -5 tooltip = JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_tt }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity = 10 tooltip = JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_tt }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity = 5 tooltip = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_tt }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity = -5 tooltip = JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity_tt }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity = -5 tooltip = JAP_tohokai_popularity_tt }
		}
		JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
	}
}

		name = NW_JAP.266.a

			limit = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_Hiranuma_Kiichiro }

		}

			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Hiranuma_Kiichiro
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = "POLITICS_HIRANUMA_KIICHIRO_DESC"
					ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { JAP_the_hidden_schemer JAP_a_representative_of_the_old_elites }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.266.b
		if = {
			limit = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_Fusanosuke_Kuhara }
			promote_character = JAP_Fusanosuke_Kuhara
		}

# FROM Япония предлагает перемирие
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.269
	title = NW_JAP.269.t
	desc = NW_JAP.269.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_101_269_271_272
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.269" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.269.a
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.40 days = 1 } }
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { OR = { original_tag = FROM is_in_faction_with = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } }
			white_peace = { tag = ROOT }
		}
		FROM = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = { NOT = { state = 525 state = 527 state = 528 state = 529 state = 530 state = 531 state = 532 state = 533 state = 534 state = 535 state = 536 state = 471 state = 282 } }
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.269.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.271 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.269.c
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.270 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	title = NW_JAP.271.t
	desc = NW_JAP.271.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_101_269_271_272
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.271" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.271.a
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.272 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.271.b
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { OR = { original_tag = FROM is_in_faction_with = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } }
			white_peace = { tag = ROOT }
		}
		every_controlled_state = {
			limit = { NOT = { state = 528 state = 529 state = 530 state = 531 state = 532 state = 533 state = 534 state = 535 state = 536 state = 282 } }
			transfer_state_to = FROM
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" has_dlc = "Man the Guns" } }
				set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
				else = { puppet = ROOT }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.41 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.273.a
		trigger = { command_power > 49 }
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 5 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		add_command_power = -50
		JAP_Yasuhiko_Asaka = { retire = yes }
		JAP_iwane_matsui = { retire = yes }
		JAP_Heisuke_Yanagava = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = JAP_purge_of_Kodoha_members_in_the_Army_flag } }
				set_character_flag = JAP_mass_killings_in_Nanjing_flag
				effect_tooltip = { retire = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.273.b
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 15 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }

			has_global_flag = THE_MOTHER_OF_ORDER_FLAG
			has_global_flag = WORLD_OF_SPLIT_FLAG

			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hideki_Todze ruling_only = yes }

		check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 70 }

		NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_incident_with_zorge }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }
	fire_only_once = yes

		name = NW_JAP.292.a
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.293 days = 1 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.295
	title = NW_JAP.295.t
	desc = NW_JAP.295.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.295
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.295" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.295.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
		load_focus_tree = nw_japan_looser_focus
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.47 days = 1 }
			FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.297 days = 2 } }
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { OR = { is_literally_china = yes is_in_faction_with = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } }
			white_peace = { tag = ROOT }
		}
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } NOT = { original_tag = MAN } }
			ROOT = { end_puppet = PREV }
			FROM = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { OR = { is_literally_china = yes tag = KOR } }
			every_core_state = {
				limit = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
				transfer_state_to = FROM
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.295.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				enemies_strength_ratio > 2
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -6
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -4
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.296 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	id = NW_JAP.297
	title = NW_JAP.297.t
	desc = NW_JAP.297.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.297
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { any_controlled_state = { is_core_of = KOR } }
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.297" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.297.a
		every_controlled_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = KOR }
			transfer_state_to = KOR
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OR = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" has_dlc = "Man the Guns" } }
			set_autonomy = { target = KOR autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
			else = { puppet = KOR }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.297.b
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		every_controlled_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = KOR }
			transfer_state_to = KOR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.297.c
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_political_power = -35
	}
}

	title = NW_JAP.306.t
	desc = NW_JAP.306.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.306
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.306" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.306.a
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = -10 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.07 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = monarchy popularity = 0.07 }
		set_country_flag = Lord_selects_premier
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.306.b
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = -20 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.05 }
		add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = JAP_the_threat_of_radicalization_of_young_officers days = 50 }
		set_country_flag = Militaries_selects_premier 
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.306.c
		add_popularity = { ideology = monarchy popularity = 0.1 }
		add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = JAP_the_threat_of_radicalization_of_young_officers days = 125 }
		set_country_flag = Emperor_selects_premier 
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.306.d
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = -10 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = monarchy popularity = 0.05 }
		set_country_flag = New_genro_select_premier
	}
}

# Создание Лиги Восточной Азии
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.307
	title = NW_JAP.307.t
	desc = NW_JAP.307.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.307
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { 
		has_war_with = CHI 
		date < 1945.04.01
		has_completed_focus = JAP_state_of_National_Defense 
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.307" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.307.a
		add_war_support = -0.05
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = fascism } }
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.02 }
			set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = JAP_fascism_party5 name = JAP_fascism_party5 }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Kimura_Takeo
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = nichirenism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = {  }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { 
			add_stability = -0.03 
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.308 days = 90 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	hidden = yes
    id = NW_JAP.312
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): hidden event NW_JAP.312" }
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
					has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hideki_Todze ruling_only = yes }
					has_country_flag = JAP_manchurian_was_scolded_flag
				}
				has_war_with = CHI
			}
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.314 }
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.313 }
		}
	}
}

# Ишивара берёт руководство на себя

	id = NW_JAP.313
	title = NW_JAP.313.t
	desc = NW_JAP.313.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.313
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.313" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.313.a
		if = {
			limit = { JAP_Kimura_Takeo = { can_be_country_leader = yes } }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = nichirenism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { JAP_leader_of_the_Manchurian_faction JAP_national_hero }
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_character = JAP_Hideki_Todze 
				has_character = JAP_yoshijiro_umezu
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = NW_JAP.608 }
		}
	}
}

# CHI \\ Делегация из Японии
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.315
	title = NW_JAP.315.t
	desc = NW_JAP.315.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.315
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.315" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.315.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				enemies_strength_ratio > 2
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -6
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -4
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.53 days = 1 } }
		FROM = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				white_peace = { tag = PREV }
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } NOT = { original_tag = MAN } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
		MAN = {
			if = {
				limit = { exists = yes }
				ROOT = { NW_remove_unrecognized_effect = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.315.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.316 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	id = NW_JAP.319
	title = NW_JAP.319.t
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.319.d.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes } } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.319.d.b
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.319
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_318_event_flag }
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.319" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.319.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = JAP_take_a_tough_anti_war_stance }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.320 days = 10 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.321 days = 10 }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = NW_JAP_319_event_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.319.b
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes } }
		set_country_flag = NW_JAP_319_b_event_flag
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.321 days = 10 } }
		set_country_flag = NW_JAP_319_event_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.319.c

# Подготовительный комитет
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.323
	title = NW_JAP.323.t
	desc = NW_JAP.323.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.323
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.323" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.323.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = JAP_people_Savings_Promotion_Company }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.324 days = 10 }	#Окружение Коноэ поддерживает Накано
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = JAP_take_a_tough_anti_war_stance }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag } }
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.325 days = 10 }	#Новая Обновленческая партия сформирована
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.326 days = 10 }	#Напряжённость в переговорах
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_take_a_tough_anti_war_stance }
					has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.326 days = 10 }	#Напряжённость в переговорах
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.327 days = 10 }	#Нерешённый вопрос
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.323.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes }
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_319_b_event_flag
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag } }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.326 days = 10 }	#Напряжённость в переговорах
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.327 days = 10 }	#Нерешённый вопрос
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.323.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes }
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_319_c_event_flag
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag } }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.326 days = 10 }	#Напряжённость в переговорах
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.325 days = 10 }	#Новая Обновленческая партия сформирована
			}
		}
	}
}

# Окружение Коноэ поддерживает Накано
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.324
	title = NW_JAP.324.t
	desc = NW_JAP.324.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.324
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.324" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.324.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = JAP_take_a_tough_anti_war_stance }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag } }
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.325 days = 10 }	#Новая Обновленческая партия сформирована
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.328 days = 10 }	#Коллективное руководство новой партией
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag }
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.326 days = 10 }	#Напряжённость в переговорах
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.327 days = 10 }		#Нерешённый вопрос
			}
		}
	}
}

# Новая обновленческая партия сформирована
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.325
	title = NW_JAP.325.t
	desc = NW_JAP.325.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.325
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.325" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.325.a
		set_country_flag = NW_JAP_325_event_flag
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission }
			set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = JAP_fascism_party6 name = JAP_fascism_party6 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = NW_JAP_325_event_tt
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp = JAP_tohokai_popularity }
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_shakai_taishuto_popularity_temp = JAP_shakai_taishuto_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity = JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp tooltip = NW_JAP_325_toh_tt }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity = JAP_shakai_taishuto_popularity_temp tooltip = NW_JAP_325_st_tt }
			clear_variable = JAP_tohokai_popularity
			clear_variable = JAP_shakai_taishuto_popularity
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_320_event_flag }
				custom_effect_tooltip = NW_JAP_325_event_tt_2
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp = JAP_small_parties_popularity }
				divide_temp_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp
				add_to_variable = { JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity = JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp tooltip = NW_JAP_325_sp_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity = JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp }
			}
			add_to_variable = { JAP_currently_num_parties = -1 }
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.329 days = 25 } }		#Противовес Какушин Шинто
		}
	}
}

		name = NW_JAP.326.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag
						democratic > 0.6
					}
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.330 days = 1 }				#Коноэ возглавит Новую Обновленческую партию
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag }
						has_completed_focus = JAP_parliamentary_elections
						democratic > 0.6
					}
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.330 days = 1 }				#Коноэ возглавит Новую Обновленческую партию
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.331 days = 1 }						#Совместное заявление
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.334
	title = NW_JAP.334.t
	desc = NW_JAP.334.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.334
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_war = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity }
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.331" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.334.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.03 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission
				check_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity > 0 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = NW_JAP_334_event_tt
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp = JAP_tohokai_popularity }
			divide_temp_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp = 2 }
			round_temp_variable = JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp
			add_to_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity = JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp tooltip = JAP_small_parties_popularity_tt }
			subtract_from_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity = JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp }
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Судьба Фусаносукэ Кухары
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.340
	title = NW_JAP.340.t
	desc = NW_JAP.340.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.340
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { has_country_flag = JAP_arrange_a_tribunal_over_the_indirectly_guilty_COMPLETE_flag }
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.340" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.340.a
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 3 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.341 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.340.b
		add_political_power = -10
	}
}

# Инновационный альянс Риккен Сэйюкай
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.342
	title = NW_JAP.342.t
	desc = NW_JAP.342.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.342
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { has_country_flag = JAP_arrange_a_tribunal_over_the_indirectly_guilty_COMPLETE_flag }
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.342" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.342.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_341_event_flag }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.382 days = 30 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.345 days = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Пульсар
country_event = {
	hidden = yes
    id = NW_JAP.382
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): hidden event NW_JAP.382" }
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = JAP_pandering_to_the_pro_war_faction }
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.343 }				#Судзуки назначает новое руководство Сэйюкай
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.344 }				#Накадзима становится новым президентом Сэйюкай
		}
	}
}

# Альянс за реформы покидает Сэйюкай
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.348
	title = NW_JAP.348.t
	desc = NW_JAP.348.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.348
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.348" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.348.a
		set_country_flag = NW_JAP_348_event_flag
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.349 days = 40 } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission }
			custom_effect_tooltip = NW_JAP_348_event_tt
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_temp = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity }
			divide_temp_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_temp = 3 }
			round_temp_variable = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_temp
			add_to_variable = { JAP_innovation_alliance_popularity = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_temp tooltip = JAP_innovation_alliance_popularity_tt }
			divide_temp_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_temp = -1 }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_temp tooltip = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_tt }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_currently_num_parties = 1 }
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Раскол Риккен Сэйюкай
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.350
	title = NW_JAP.350.t
	desc = NW_JAP.350.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.350
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.350" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.350.a
		set_country_flag = JAP_split_of_seukai_flag
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission }
			custom_effect_tooltip = NW_JAP_350_event_tt
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_temp = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity }
			divide_temp_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_temp = 2 }
			round_temp_variable = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_temp
			add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_temp tooltip = JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_tt }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_temp tooltip = JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_tt }
			clear_variable = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity
			add_to_variable = { JAP_currently_num_parties = 1 }
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.351 days = 5 }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.352 days = 20 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Нейтральная фракция
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.351
	title = NW_JAP.351.t
	desc = NW_JAP.351.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.351
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.351" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.351.a
		set_temp_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_temp = JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity }
		divide_temp_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_temp = 10 }
		round_temp_variable = JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_temp
		set_temp_variable = { JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_temp = JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity }
		divide_temp_variable = { JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_temp = 10 }
		round_temp_variable = JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_temp
		set_temp_variable = { JAP_sum_of_two_parties = 0 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_sum_of_two_parties = JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_temp }
		add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_sum_of_two_parties = JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_temp }
		add_to_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity = JAP_sum_of_two_parties tooltip = JAP_small_parties_popularity_tt }
		divide_temp_variable = { JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_temp = -1 }
		divide_temp_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_temp = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity = JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_temp tooltip = JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_tt }
		add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity = JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_temp tooltip = JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_tt }
		JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
	}
}

# Пульсар
country_event = {
	hidden = yes
    id = NW_JAP.352
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): hidden event NW_JAP.352" }
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { neutrality > party_popularity@democratic }
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.383 }				#Кухара возглавляет ортодоксальную Риккен Сэйюкай
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.353 }				#Хатояма возглавляет ортодоксальную Риккен Сэйюкай
		}
	}
}

# Усиление провоенной агитации Риккен Сэйюкай
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.359
	title = NW_JAP.359.t
	desc = NW_JAP.359.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.359
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_purge_of_Toseiha_members_in_the_Army_country_flag }
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_347_event_flag
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_358_event_flag
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_344_event_flag
		}
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.359" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.359.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NW_JAP_347_event_flag
					has_country_flag = NW_JAP_358_event_flag
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity = 10 tooltip = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_tt }
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_shinshinto_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_shinshinto_popularity = -10 tooltip = JAP_shinshinto_popularity_tt }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity = -10 tooltip = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_tt }
			}
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_344_event_flag }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity = 7 tooltip = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_tt }
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_shinshinto_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_shinshinto_popularity = -7 tooltip = JAP_shinshinto_popularity_tt }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity = -7 tooltip = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_tt }
			}
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.385
	title = NW_JAP.385.t
	desc = NW_JAP.385.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.385
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.385" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.385.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_power_balance = { id = JAP_invite_farmers_power_balance } }
			remove_power_balance = { id = JAP_invite_farmers_power_balance }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Gondo_Seike ruling_only = yes } }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_Jinzaburo_Masaki }
					remove_country_leader_role = {
						character = JAP_Jinzaburo_Masaki
						ideology = monarchy_ideology
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Jinzaburo_Masaki
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = agrarian_nationalism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { JAP_hated_by_political_elites JAP_Conflict_with_the_Manchurian_Faction JAP_the_leader_of_Kodoha }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.386 days = 1 } }
		}
		retire_character = JAP_Gondo_Seike
	}
}

		name = NW_JAP.384.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_300_event_flag
			has_completed_focus = JAP_condemn_the_movement_in_one_party
			
		}
		set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.1 }
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_war_support = -0.1
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.384.b
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = JAP_preparation_of_Ugaki_heir }
		set_country_flag = JAP_Abe_office_UNLOCK_flag
		effect_tooltip = { unlock_national_focus = JAP_Abe_office }
		retire_country_leader = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_189_c_event_flag }
			promote_character = JAP_Dziro_Minami
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party13 name = JAP_neutrality_party13 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_189_b_event_flag }
			promote_character = JAP_kuniaki_koiso
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party14 name = JAP_neutrality_party14 }
		}
		else = {
			promote_character = JAP_Nobuyuki_Abe
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party12 name = JAP_neutrality_party12 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.384.c
		promote_character = JAP_Hirota_Koki
		set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party6 name = JAP_neutrality_party6 }
	}
}

	desc = NW_JAP.401.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.401
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.401"
		hidden_effect = {
			save_event_target_as = alliance_applicant
			FROM = { save_event_target_as = alliance_inviter }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.401.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_war = no
				FROM = { has_war = yes }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = alliance_applicant@ROOT
			FROM = { set_country_flag = alliance_inviter@ROOT }
			news_event = { id = news.289 hours = 12 }
		}
		FROM = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = FROM
			value = 200
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.401.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 65 }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 35 }
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 5 }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value < 35 }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value < 65 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_war = yes
				FROM = { has_war = no }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.402 days = 1 } }
	}
}

		check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 7 }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_purge_of_Toseiha_members_in_the_Army_country_flag }
		can_declare_war_on = HCP
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.425" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.425.a
		HCP = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.404 days = 1 } }
	}
}

# Отмена монархии
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.434
	title = NW_JAP.434.t
	desc = NW_JAP.434.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.434
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.434" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.434.a
		set_country_flag = NW_JAP_434_event_flag
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Iwasaburo_Takano
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = socialism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {  }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_Seva }
			remove_ideas = JAP_Seva
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Seva }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Seva
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Seva1 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Seva1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Seva2 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Seva2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Seva3 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Seva3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_Reiva }
			remove_ideas = JAP_Reiva
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva1 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva2 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva3 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva3
		}
		add_ideas = JAP_mass_defiance_of_the_occupation_idea
		set_variable = { JAP_power_of_resistance_var = 6 }
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = JAP_the_fight_against_the_monarchist_underground_category
		activate_mission = JAP_discontent_of_the_peasants_mission
		activate_mission = JAP_activities_of_religious_radicals_mission
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = global.majors
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			activate_mission = JAP_activities_of_communist_underground_mission
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_major = yes
					has_government = communism
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.452 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = anarchism }
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = global.majors
					has_government = anarchism
				}
			}
			activate_mission = JAP_activities_of_anarchist_underground_mission
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_major = yes
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.453 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Формирование Реформированного правительства Китайской Республики I
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.442
	title = NW_JAP.442.t
	desc = NW_JAP.442.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.442
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.442" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.442.a
		create_dynamic_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			add_political_power = 100
			transfer_state = 613
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
					set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_subject }
					else = { puppet = PREV }
				}
				set_nationality = { target_country = PREV character = CHI_Tang_Shaoyi }
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_reformed_government_of_the_republic_of_china
			if = { 
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Tang_Shaoyi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nationalism_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = neutrality }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Tang_Shaoyi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = monarchy }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Tang_Shaoyi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {

					}

			add_political_power = 100
			transfer_state = 613
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
					set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_subject }
					else = { puppet = PREV }
				}
				set_nationality = { target_country = PREV character = CHI_Tang_Shaoyi }
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_reformed_government_of_the_republic_of_china
			if = { 
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Tang_Shaoyi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nationalism_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = neutrality }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Tang_Shaoyi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}

			}
			else_if = {

				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Tang_Shaoyi

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.443
	title = NW_JAP.443.t
	desc = NW_JAP.443.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.442
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.443" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.443.a
		create_dynamic_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			add_political_power = 100
			transfer_state = 613
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
					set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_subject }
					else = { puppet = PREV }
				}
				set_nationality = { target_country = PREV character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi }
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_reformed_government_of_the_republic_of_china
			if = { 
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nationalism_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = neutrality }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = monarchy }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = monarchy_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = democratic }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = liberalism
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = technocracy }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = technocracy_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.443.b
		create_dynamic_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			add_political_power = 100
			transfer_state = 613
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
					set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_subject }
					else = { puppet = PREV }
				}
				set_nationality = { target_country = PREV character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi }
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_reformed_government_of_the_republic_of_china
			if = { 
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nationalism_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = neutrality }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = monarchy }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = monarchy_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = democratic }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = liberalism
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = technocracy }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_Liang_Hongzhi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = technocracy_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}
}

# Четыре рукопожатия
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.444
	title = NW_JAP.444.t
	desc = NW_JAP.444.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP. # TODO !!
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.444" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.444.a
		country_event = { id = NW_JAP.445 hours = 12 }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_create_a_brotherhood_op
				target = ROOT
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_create_a_brotherhood_op
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.445
	title = NW_JAP.445.t
	desc = NW_JAP.445.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.445
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.445" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.445.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.03 }
		add_country_leader_trait = JAP_supporter_of_the_ideas_of_coudenhove_kalergi
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					has_opinion_modifier = JAP_create_a_brotherhood_op
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_create_a_brotherhood_op
				target = ROOT
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_create_a_brotherhood_op
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.59 days = 3 } }
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.434 days = 1 } }		
	}

		name = NW_JAP.446.b

	}
