# Восстание крестьян
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.448
	title = NW_JAP.448.t
	desc = NW_JAP.448.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.448
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.448"
		hidden_effect = {
			MPJ = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_country_with_original_tag = {
							original_tag_to_check = ROOT 
							has_character = JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi
						}
					}
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = ROOT
							has_character = JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi
						}
						JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi = {
							set_nationality = PREV.PREV
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = absolute_monarchy
									expire = "1965.1.1.1"
									traits = {  }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					promote_character = JAP_Takusiro_Hattori
				}
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Showa Defenders" } }
					division_template = {
						name = "Showa Defenders"
						is_locked = yes
						division_names_group = JAP_INF_01
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					every_core_state = { add_core_of = PREV.PREV }
					set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = num_controlled_states }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { JAP_power_of_resistance_var > 7 } }
						divide_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 1.66 }
						PREV = { set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 20 } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { JAP_power_of_resistance_var > 3 } }
						divide_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 2 }
						PREV = { set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 13 } }
					}
					else = {
						divide_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 3 }
						PREV = { set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 8 } }
					}
					while_loop_effect = {
						limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp > 0 } }
						add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = -1 }
						random_controlled_state = {
							transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
					PREV = {
						while_loop_effect = {
							limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp > 0 } }
							add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = -1 }
							random_controlled_state = {
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Righteous Army\" division_template = \"Showa Defenders\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
									owner = PREV
									count = 1
								}
							}
						}
					}
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = PREV
						size = 0.5
						stockpile_ratio = 0.4
						army_ratio = 0.4
						air_ratio = 0.4
						navy_ratio = 0.4
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
							is_country_leader = no
							is_advisor = no
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = civil_war }
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = ROOT NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					PREV = { add_civil_war_target = PREV }
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
				every_enemy_country = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
							controller = { tag = PREV.PREV }
						}
						teleport_armies = {
							limit = { tag = PREV }
							to_state_array = controlled_states
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.448.a		
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.448.b
		MPJ = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

# Восстание секты Нитирэн
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.449
	title = NW_JAP.449.t
	desc = NW_JAP.449.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.448
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.449"
		hidden_effect = {
			FPJ = {
				transfer_state = 535
				set_province_controller = 4100
				set_province_controller = 7016
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						has_character = JAP_Nisse_Inoye
					}
					set_nationality = { target_country = PREV character = JAP_Nisse_Inoye }
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						has_character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
					}
					set_nationality = { target_country = PREV character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara }									
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Nisse_Inoye
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nichirenism
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Nithirenists" } }
					division_template = {
						name = "Nithirenists"
						is_locked = yes
						division_names_group = JAP_INF_01
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 4 }
				while_loop_effect = {
					limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp > 0 } }
					add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = -1 }
					random_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Nithirenists\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
							owner = PREV
							count = 1
						}
					}
				}				
				ROOT = {
					every_core_state = { add_core_of = PREV.PREV }
					declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = civil_war }
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = ROOT NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					PREV = { add_civil_war_target = PREV }
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
				every_enemy_country = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
							controller = { tag = PREV.PREV }
						}
						teleport_armies = {
							limit = { tag = PREV }
							to_state_array = controlled_states
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.449.a		
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.449.b
		FPJ = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

# Восстание коммунистов
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.450
	title = NW_JAP.450.t
	desc = NW_JAP.450.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.448
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.450"
		hidden_effect = {
			CPJ = {
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_political_and_religious_freedoms } }
					ROOT = {
						JAP_Kyuichi_Tokuda = {
							set_nationality = PREV.PREV
							promote_character = yes
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_country_with_original_tag = {
							original_tag_to_check = ROOT 
							has_character = JAP_Kenzo_Yamamoto
						}
					}
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = ROOT
							has_character = JAP_Kenzo_Yamamoto
						}
						JAP_Kenzo_Yamamoto = {
							set_nationality = PREV.PREV
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = marxism
									expire = "1965.1.1.1"
									traits = {  }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					promote_character = JAP_Sanzo_Nosaka
				}
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Red Brigades" } }
					division_template = {
						name = "Red Brigades"
						is_locked = yes
						division_names_group = JAP_INF_01
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_commi_var > 4 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 4 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 4 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_commi_var > 2 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 3 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 3 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_commi_var > 0 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 2 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 2 }
					}
					else = {
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 1 }
					}
					while_loop_effect = {
						limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp > 0 } }
						add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = -1 }
						random_controlled_state = {
							transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 3 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = ROOT.JAP_num_helpls_for_commi_var }
				while_loop_effect = {
					limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp > 0 } }
					add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = -1 }
					random_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Red Brigades\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
							owner = PREV
							count = 1
						}
					}
				}			
				ROOT = {
					every_core_state = { add_core_of = PREV.PREV }
					declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = civil_war }
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = ROOT NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					PREV = { add_civil_war_target = PREV }
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
				every_enemy_country = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
							controller = { tag = PREV.PREV }
						}
						teleport_armies = {
							limit = { tag = PREV }
							to_state_array = controlled_states
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.450.a		
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.450.b
		CPJ = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

# Восстание коммунистов
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.451
	title = NW_JAP.451.t
	desc = NW_JAP.451.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.448
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.451"
		hidden_effect = {
			APJ = {
				promote_character = JAP_Sanzo_Nosaka
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Red Brigades" } }
					division_template = {
						name = "Red Brigades"
						is_locked = yes
						division_names_group = JAP_INF_01
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_anarchists_var > 4 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 4 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 4 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_anarchists_var > 2 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 3 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 3 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_anarchists_var > 0 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 2 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 2 }
					}
					else = {
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 1 }
					}
					while_loop_effect = {
						limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp > 0 } }
						add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = -1 }
						random_controlled_state = {
							transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 3 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = ROOT.JAP_num_helpls_for_anarchists_var }
				while_loop_effect = {
					limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp > 0 } }
					add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = -1 }
					random_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Red Brigades\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
							owner = PREV
							count = 1
						}
					}
				}			
				ROOT = {
					every_core_state = { add_core_of = PREV.PREV }
					declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = civil_war }
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = ROOT NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					PREV = { add_civil_war_target = PREV }
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
				every_enemy_country = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
							controller = { tag = PREV.PREV }
						}
						teleport_armies = {
							limit = { tag = PREV }
							to_state_array = controlled_states
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.451.a		
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.451.b
		APJ = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

		}

				ideology = pure_socialism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"

			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.454.b
		trigger = { has_character = JAP_Nobuhito }
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Nobuhito
			promote_leader = yes

			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.454.c
		trigger = { has_character = JAP_Takahito }
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Takahito
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = monarchy_ideology
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {  }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.454.d
		trigger = { has_character = JAP_Prince_Naruhito }
		JAP_Prince_Naruhito = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_ideology_group = monarchy } }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes

						ideology = monarchy_ideology

			}
		}
	}

			has_war_with = JAP
		}
	}
	option = {

				has_government = communism
				has_government = trozkism
				has_government = anarchism
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
			has_government = fascism
		}
	}
	option = {

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = NW_JAP.485.a
		set_country_flag = JAP_anti_soviet_alliance_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.65 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.492 days = 3 }
		}
		add_to_faction = FROM
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = JAP_anti_soviet_alliance_flag
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_discontent_of_the_military_mission }
				add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = JAP_discontent_of_the_military_mission days = 200 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_anti_soviet_alliance_op
				target = ROOT
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_anti_soviet_alliance_op
				target = FROM
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.485.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.493 hours = 12 } }
	}
}

		text = NW_JAP.499.d.a

			FROM = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_498_a_flag }
			SOV = {
				OR = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_war_with = FROM
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.499.d.b
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_498_a_flag }
			SOV = {
				has_civil_war = no
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = FROM
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.499.d.c
		trigger = { FROM = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_498_b_flag } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.499.d.d
		trigger = { FROM = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_498_c_flag } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.499" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.499.a

			NOT = { tag = FROM }
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NW_JAP_498_c_flag
					has_country_flag = NW_JAP_498_a_flag
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = NW_JAP.500 hours = 12 }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.499.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = FROM }
			FROM = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_498_b_flag }

	id = NW_JAP.513
	title = NW_JAP.513.t
	desc = NW_JAP.513.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.513" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.513.a
		country_event = NW_JAP.514
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SOV }
			diplomatic_relation = { country = JAP relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes }
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = { diplomatic_relation = { country = FROM relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_discontent_of_the_military_mission }
				add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = JAP_discontent_of_the_military_mission days = 50 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.70 days = 1 }
				ENG = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.516 days = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.516 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = NW_JAP.521
	title = NW_JAP.521.t
	desc = NW_JAP.521.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.

		trigger = { check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var < 40 } }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 15 } }

		}

			FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.526 hours = 12 } }
		}
	}

	}

	id = NW_JAP.524
	title = NW_JAP.524.t
	desc = NW_JAP.524.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.524" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.524.a
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 5 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
		#TODO: CCG было признано со стороны JAP
		CHI = {
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.522 hours = 12 }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.525 days = 5 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.524.b
		trigger = { has_political_power > 50 }
		add_political_power = -50
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_discontent_of_the_military_mission }
			add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = JAP_discontent_of_the_military_mission days = -30 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
		}
		CHI = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.526 hours = 12 } }
	}
}

# CHI Согласие японцев
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.526
	title = NW_JAP.526.t
	desc = NW_JAP.526.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.526" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.526.a
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.71 days = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			dismantle_faction = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
		}
		FROM = {
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { is_literally_china = yes NOT = { original_tag = MAN } }
				PREV = { end_puppet = PREV }
				if = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = PREV }
					custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
					leave_faction = yes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				white_peace = { tag = PREV }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_line_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = NW_USA_treaty_on_trade_and_navigation_with_japan_idea } }
			add_ideas = NW_USA_treaty_on_trade_and_navigation_with_japan_idea
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.540.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.537 hours = 12 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.556
	title = NW_JAP.556.t
	desc = NW_JAP.556.desc
	trigger = { 
		OR = { 
			has_completed_focus = JAP_Hirota_Koki_office  
			has_completed_focus = JAP_new_Okada_government 
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.556
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.556" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.556.a
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				AND = { 
					has_completed_focus = JAP_Hirota_Koki_office 
					has_war = yes
				}
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = JAP_new_Okada_government  
					NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Keisuke_Okada ruling_only = yes } }
				}
			}	
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.556.b
		trigger = { 
			has_completed_focus = JAP_Hirota_Koki_office 
			has_war = no
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.556.c
		trigger = { 
			has_completed_focus = JAP_new_Okada_government 
			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Keisuke_Okada ruling_only = yes }
			}
		add_political_power = -40 
		add_stability = -0.01
		add_power_balance_value = {
			id = JAP_new_Okada_government_power_balance
			value = -0.1
			tooltip_side = JAP_supporters_of_democracy
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.556.d
		trigger = { 
			has_completed_focus = JAP_new_Okada_government 
			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Keisuke_Okada ruling_only = yes }
		}
		add_stability = -0.03

	}

		trigger = { has_country_flag = Privy_council_selects_premier }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.571.d.a 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Lord_and_Elders_select_premier } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.571.d.a 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Elders_selects_premier } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.571.d.a 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Privy_council_selects_premier } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.571
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.571" }

					has_country_flag = Privy_council_selects_premier
				}
			}

		}
	}

# Всем офицерам и рядовым Императорской армии 
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.584
	title = NW_JAP.584.t
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.584.d.a 
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = JAP_last_war }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.584.d.b 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_last_war } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.584
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.584" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.584.a
		set_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 0 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt2 }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = JAP_gekokujo } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_subjugate_the_military_to_the_imperial_will_tt
			hidden_effect = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = JAP_gekokujo } }
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_3
				add_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2
				add_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1 }
			remove_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1
		}
	}
}

			value = -0.05

		}
		GER = { 
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_critic_on_mainkampf_op
				target = ROOT
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_critic_on_mainkampf_op

			} 
		}
	}

# Новые идеологические позиции Ишивары
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.594
	title = NW_JAP.594.t
	desc = NW_JAP.594.d
	trigger = { 
		date > 1948.11.10
		OR = { 
			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara ruling_only = yes }
			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Seishiro_Itagaki ruling_only = yes }
			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Kimura_Takeo ruling_only = yes }
		}
		has_character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
		has_war = no 
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.594
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.594" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.594.a
		add_power_balance_value = {
			id = JAP_Ishiwara_power_balance
			value = -0.1
			tooltip_side = JAP_farmers
		}
		add_political_power = -40 
		add_war_support = -0.15 
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.594.b
		trigger = { JAP_Ishiwara_power_balance > -0.15	}
		add_power_balance_value = {
			id = JAP_Ishiwara_power_balance
			value = 0.03
			tooltip_side = JAP_nichirenists
		}
		add_political_power = -50
	}
}

# Смерть Кандзи Ишивары
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.598
	title = NW_JAP.598.t
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.598.desc.a 
		trigger = { 
			OR = { 
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara ruling_only = yes } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Seishiro_Itagaki ruling_only = yes } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Kimura_Takeo ruling_only = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.598.desc.b 
		trigger = { 
			OR = { 
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_formation_of_the_highest_culture }
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_power_through_science }
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_fulfill_nichiren_prediction }
			}
			OR = { 
				has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara ruling_only = yes }
				has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Seishiro_Itagaki ruling_only = yes }
				has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Kimura_Takeo ruling_only = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.598
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.598" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.598.a
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara ruling_only = yes } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Seishiro_Itagaki ruling_only = yes } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Kimura_Takeo ruling_only = yes } }
			}
		}
		retire_character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.598.b
		trigger = { 
			has_completed_focus = JAP_formation_of_the_highest_culture
		}
		retire_character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Kimura_Takeo
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = "POLITICS_KIMURA_TAKEO_DESC"
				ideology = social_liberalism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.598.c
		trigger = { 
			has_completed_focus = JAP_power_through_science
		}
		retire_character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Seishiro_Itagaki
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = "POLITICS_SEISHIRO_ITAGAKI_DESC"
				ideology = state_of_national_defense
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.598.d
		trigger = { 
			has_completed_focus = JAP_fulfill_nichiren_prediction
		}
		retire_character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = "POLITICS_MASANOBU_CUDZI_DESC"
					ideology = nichirenism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { 
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Seishiro_Itagaki
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = "POLITICS_SEISHIRO_ITAGAKI_DESC"
					ideology = nichirenism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { }
				}
			}	
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.598.e
		trigger = { 
			has_power_balance = { id = JAP_Ishiwara_power_balance }
			power_balance_value = { id = JAP_Ishiwara_power_balance value < -0.5 }
		}
		retire_character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Kimura_Takeo
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = "POLITICS_KIMURA_TAKEO_DESC"
				ideology = social_liberalism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.598.f
		trigger = { 
			has_power_balance = { id = JAP_Ishiwara_power_balance }
			power_balance_value = { id = JAP_Ishiwara_power_balance value < 0.5 }
			power_balance_value = { id = JAP_Ishiwara_power_balance value > -0.5 }
		}
		retire_character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Seishiro_Itagaki
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = "POLITICS_SEISHIRO_ITAGAKI_DESC"
				ideology = state_of_national_defense
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.598.g
		trigger = { 
			has_power_balance = { id = JAP_Ishiwara_power_balance }
			power_balance_value = { id = JAP_Ishiwara_power_balance value > 0.5 }
		}
		retire_character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = "POLITICS_MASANOBU_CUDZI_DESC"
					ideology = nichirenism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { 
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Seishiro_Itagaki
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = "POLITICS_SEISHIRO_ITAGAKI_DESC"
					ideology = nichirenism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { }
				}
			}	
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
	trigger = { 
		has_character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_State_of_National_Defense }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_purge_of_Toseiha_members_in_the_Army_country_flag }

	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.600.a
		trigger = { 
			OR = { 
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = MAN_destruction_of_hopes_for_paradise }
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = MAN_tsuji_restores_concordia_association }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_power_balance_value = {
			id = MAN_power_balance
			value = -0.05
			tooltip_side = MAN_reform_officers_bop
		}
		set_country_flag = MAN_Ishiwara_comeback_flag
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.601 days = 100 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.600.b
		trigger = { 
			has_completed_focus = MAN_destruction_of_hopes_for_paradise 
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.601 days = 25 } }
		set_country_flag = MAN_Ishiwara_comeback_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.600.c
		trigger = { 
			has_completed_focus = MAN_tsuji_restores_concordia_association 	
		}
		set_country_flag = MAN_Ishiwara_comeback_flag
		add_political_power = 30
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.607

	desc = NW_JAP.607.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.607
	is_triggered_only = yes

			NOT = { has_completed_focus = MAN_destruction_of_hopes_for_paradise }

# Роспуск партий 
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.612
	title = NW_JAP.612.t
	desc = NW_JAP.612.d
	trigger = { 
		
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.612
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.612" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.612.a
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				OR = { 
					has_country_flag = NW_JAP_346_event_flag 
					has_country_flag = NW_JAP_356_event_flag 
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_358_event_flag } 
				NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_shinshinto_was_created_flag }
				has_war = no
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_Jinzaburo_Masaki_office }				
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.614 days = 5 }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.617 days = 8}
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.624 days = 14}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					OR = { 
						NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_346_event_flag } 
						NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_356_event_flag }
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.613 days = 1 } }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					OR = { 
						has_country_flag = NW_JAP_346_event_flag 
						has_country_flag = NW_JAP_356_event_flag 
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_358_event_flag }
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.614 days = 5 } }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = JAP_split_of_seukai_flag }
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.615 days = 3 } }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_shinshinto_was_created_flag } }
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.617 days = 10} }
			}
			else = {
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.618 days = 7} }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_shinshinto_was_created_flag } }
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.620 days = 6 } }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = JAP_shinshinto_was_created_flag }
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.621 days = 6 } }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_shinshinto_was_created_flag }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_320_event_flag }
				}
				hidden_effect =  { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.622 days = 2 } }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_332_event_flag }
					has_country_flag = JAP_shinshinto_was_created_flag
				} 
				hidden_effect =  { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.623 days = 15 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

				USA = { 
					NOT = { surrender_progress > 0 }

				}
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_promote_loyal_people }
			}
			country_event = NW_JAP.637
		}
		else = { 
			country_event = NW_JAP.638
		}
	}

# Инцидент с газовой бомбой
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.637
	title = NW_JAP.637.t
	desc = NW_JAP.637.d
	trigger = { 
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.637" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.637.a
		news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.82 hours = 6 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = dead_character
		show_ideas_tooltip = JAP_Hideki_Todze
		hidden_effect = { 
			retire_character = JAP_Hideki_Todze 
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_Prince_Naruhito } }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Prince_Naruhito
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { JAP_bad_reputation_in_the_imperial_house JAP_liberal_imperialist JAP_a_mad_political_schemer }
				}
			}
			else = { promote_character = JAP_Prince_Naruhito }
		}
		set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party22 name = JAP_neutrality_party22 }
	}
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.637.b
		news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.82 hours = 6 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = dead_character
		show_ideas_tooltip = JAP_Hideki_Todze
		hidden_effect = { 
			retire_character = JAP_Hideki_Todze 
		}
		if = {
			limit = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_kuniaki_koiso }
			promote_character = JAP_kuniaki_koiso
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_kuniaki_koiso
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = {  }
				}
			}
		}
		set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party14 name = JAP_neutrality_party14 }
	}
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.637.c
		news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.82 hours = 6 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = dead_character
		show_ideas_tooltip = JAP_Hideki_Todze
		hidden_effect = { 
			retire_character = JAP_Hideki_Todze 
		}
		if = {
			limit = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_Mitsumasa_Yonai }
			promote_character = JAP_Mitsumasa_Yonai
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Mitsumasa_Yonai
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { JAP_the_Emperor_confidant JAP_a_favorite_of_women JAP_Sake_is_Enai_Enai_is_sake JAP_loves_Russian_culture }
				}
			}		
		}
		set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party11 name = JAP_neutrality_party11 }
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_TEMP = 0 }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_TEMP }
					tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_check_tt
				}
			}
			add_ideas = JAP_the_heaviest_conflict_between_army_and_navy_idea
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.642
	title = NW_JAP.642.t
	desc = NW_JAP.642.d
	trigger = { 
		
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.642" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.642.a
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				OR = { 
					NOT = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1 }
					NOT = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2 }
					NOT = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_3 }
				}
				check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 0 }
			}
			add_ideas = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_3
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				OR = { 
					NOT = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1 }
					NOT = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2 }
					NOT = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_3 }
				}
				check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 0 }
			}
			add_ideas = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2
		}
		set_country_flag = JAP_treatment_of_war_prisoners_flag
	}
}

# Выходки Масанобу Цудзи
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.643
	title = NW_JAP.643.t
	desc = NW_JAP.643.d
	trigger = { 
		has_character = JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi
		any_enemy_country = { 
			capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe }
			surrender_progress > 0
		}
		tag = JAP
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.643" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.643.a
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 5 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		if = { 
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2
				add_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_3
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1
				add_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				OR = { 
					NOT = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1 }
					NOT = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2 }
					NOT = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_3 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.652
	title = NW_JAP.652.t
	desc = NW_JAP.652.d
	trigger = { 
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.652" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.652.a
		if = {
			limit = { JAP_Keisuke_Okada = { has_country_leader_with_trait = JAP_psychological_tension } }
			JAP_Keisuke_Okada = { 
				swap_country_leader_traits = { 
					remove_country_leader_trait = JAP_psychological_tension
					add_country_leader_trait = JAP_morally_depressed
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { JAP_Keisuke_Okada = { has_country_leader_with_trait = JAP_morally_depressed } }
			JAP_Keisuke_Okada = { 
				swap_country_leader_traits	 = { 
					remove_country_leader_trait = JAP_morally_depressed
					add_country_leader_trait = JAP_poor_morale
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { JAP_Keisuke_Okada = { has_country_leader_with_trait = JAP_poor_morale } }
			JAP_Keisuke_Okada = { 
				swap_country_leader_traits	 = { 
					remove_country_leader_trait = JAP_poor_morale
					add_country_leader_trait = JAP_close_to_suicide
				}
			}
		}
		else = { 
			limit = { JAP_Keisuke_Okada = { has_country_leader_with_trait = JAP_close_to_suicide } }
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.653 hours = 12 }
		}
	}
}

# Премьер Окада обнаружён мёртвым
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.653
	title = NW_JAP.653.t
	desc = NW_JAP.653.d
	trigger = { 
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.653" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.653.a
		kill_country_leader = yes
		remove_power_balance = { id = JAP_new_Okada_government_power_balance }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_Fumimaro_Konoe } }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Fumimaro_Konoe
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = "POLITICS_FUMIMARO_KONOE_DESC"
					ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { JAP_ambitious_political_views JAP_the_melancholic_Prince2 JAP_opponent_of_the_war_with_the_United_States }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { promote_character = JAP_Fumimaro_Konoe }
		set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party8 name = JAP_neutrality_party8 }
		activate_mission = JAP_time_to_retirement
		activate_mission = JAP_change_of_mood
	}
}

    id = NW_JAP.675
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): hidden event NW_JAP.675" }
	immediate = {
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes }
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_lead_the_conservatives }
			}
			country_event = NW_JAP.673
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_lead_the_conservatives }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_shinshinto_was_created_flag }
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_Jinzaburo_Masaki_office } # этот и следующий триггер можно заменить на проверку того произошёл ли роспуск партий но это надо обратиться к Сане
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_create_an_Association_to_Help_the_Throne }
			}
			country_event = NW_JAP.674
		}
	}
} 

# Армия тайно поддерживает Тохокай
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.676
	title = NW_JAP.676.t
	desc = NW_JAP.676.d
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_319_event_flag } #национальный фронт
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_393_flag } #итоги поездки
		has_completed_focus = JAP_manchurian_modernizes_the_army
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.676" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.676.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity = 10 tooltip = JAP_tohokai_popularity_tt }
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_shinshinto_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_shinshinto_popularity = -7 tooltip = JAP_shinshinto_popularity_tt }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity = -7 tooltip = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_tt }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity } }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity = -2 tooltip = JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_tt }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity = -1 tooltip = JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_tt }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity = -3 tooltip = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_tt }
			}
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

	title = NW_JAP.682.t
	desc = NW_JAP.682.d
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_330_event_flag } # Коноэ возглавит Новую Обновленческую партию
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_352_event_flag } # Кухара возглавляет ортодоксальную Риккен Сэйюкай
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_319_event_flag } # национальный фронт 
		has_idea = JAP_movement_for_One_Party
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.682" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.682.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission }
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_tohokai_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity = 10 tooltip = JAP_tohokai_popularity_tt }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity } }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity = -2 tooltip = JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_tt }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity = -3 tooltip = JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_tt }
			}
			else = { 
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity = -5 tooltip = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_tt }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_shinshinto_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_shinshinto_popularity = -5 tooltip = JAP_shinshinto_popularity_tt }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity = -5 tooltip = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_tt }
			}
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Потеря доверия Риккен Минсейто
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.683
	title = NW_JAP.683.t
	desc = NW_JAP.683.d
	trigger = { 
		has_war = yes 
		has_completed_focus = JAP_take_a_tough_anti_war_stance
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.683" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.683.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission }
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_shinshinto_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_shinshinto_popularity = -8 tooltip = JAP_shinshinto_popularity_tt }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity = -8 tooltip = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_tt }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_tohokai_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity = 4 tooltip = JAP_tohokai_popularity_tt }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity } }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity = 2 tooltip = JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_tt }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity = 2 tooltip = JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_tt }
			}
			else = { 
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity = 4 tooltip = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_tt }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = NW_JAP_318_event_flag # Новая идеология Шакай Тайшуто
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = JAP_shinshinto_popularity }
					add_to_variable = { JAP_shinshinto_popularity = -4 tooltip = JAP_shinshinto_popularity_tt }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_variable = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity }
					add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity = -4 tooltip = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_tt }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = JAP_shakai_taishuto_popularity }
					add_to_variable = { JAP_shakai_taishuto_popularity = 4 tooltip = JAP_shakai_taishuto_popularity_tt }
				}
			}
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

		NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_take_a_tough_anti_war_stance }
		has_country_flag = NW_JAP_337_event_flag
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.684" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.684.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission }
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_shinshinto_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_shinshinto_popularity = 10 tooltip = JAP_shinshinto_popularity_tt }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity = 10 tooltip = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_tt }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity } }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity = -5 tooltip = JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity_tt }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity = -5 tooltip = JAP_sayukai_ortodox_popularity_tt }
			}
			else = { 
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity = -10 tooltip = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_tt }
			}
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.05 } 
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.695
	title = NW_JAP.695.t
	desc = NW_JAP.695.desc
	trigger = { 
		has_government = democratic
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.695" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.695.a
		trigger = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_popularity_of_party_var_TEMP = 49 }
				check_variable = { JAP_popularity_of_party_var > JAP_popularity_of_party_var_TEMP }
				tooltip = JAP_popularity_of_party_var_check_tt
			}
			#check_variable = { JAP_popularity_of_party_var > JAP_popularity_of_party_var_TEMP }
			#tooltip = JAP_popularity_of_party_var_check_tt
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.03 }
		add_political_power = 30
		remove_ideas = JAP_high_unity_of_rikken_Seyukai_idea
		remove_ideas = JAP_sufficient_unity_of_rikken_Seyukai_idea
		remove_ideas = JAP_low_unity_of_rikken_Seyukai_idea
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.695.b
		trigger = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_popularity_of_party_var_TEMP = 50 }
				check_variable = { JAP_popularity_of_party_var < JAP_popularity_of_party_var_TEMP }
				tooltip = JAP_popularity_of_party_var_check_tt
			}
			has_country_flag = JAP_shinshinto_was_created_flag
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_conservative_party }
		}
		set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = JAP_democratic_party2_long name = JAP_democratic_party2 }
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				OR = { 
					AND = { 
						has_country_flag = NW_JAP_318_event_flag
						has_country_flag = NW_JAP_372_event_flag
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_318_event_flag }

			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Tetsu_Katayama

					ideology = socialism

		}

				character = JAP_Inejiro_Asanuma
				promote_leader = yes

					ideology = socialism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = {  }
				}
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = JAP_high_unity_of_rikken_Seyukai_idea
		remove_ideas = JAP_sufficient_unity_of_rikken_Seyukai_idea
		remove_ideas = JAP_low_unity_of_rikken_Seyukai_idea
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.695.c
		trigger = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_popularity_of_party_var_TEMP = 50 }
				check_variable = { JAP_popularity_of_party_var < JAP_popularity_of_party_var_TEMP }
				tooltip = JAP_popularity_of_party_var_check_tt
			}

		}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.697
	title = NW_JAP.697.t
	desc = NW_JAP.697.d
	trigger = { 
		has_government = democratic
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.697" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.697.a
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
				AND = { 
					NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Ichiro_Hatoyama ruling_only = yes } }
					has_stability < 0.5 
				}
				AND = { 
					has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Ichiro_Hatoyama ruling_only = yes }
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_popularity_of_party_var_TEMP = 50 }
						check_variable = { JAP_popularity_of_party_var > JAP_popularity_of_party_var_TEMP }
						tooltip = JAP_popularity_of_party_var_check_tt
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_696_1 }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Ichiro_Kono
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = liberalism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = {  }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {

				character = JAP_Banboku_Oto
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = liberalism

					traits = {  }

			}
		}
		else = {

				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = liberalism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = {  }

					AND = { 
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Ichiro_Hatoyama ruling_only = yes } }
						has_stability < 0.5 
					}
					AND = { 
						has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Ichiro_Hatoyama ruling_only = yes }
						custom_trigger_tooltip = {
							set_temp_variable = { JAP_popularity_of_party_var_TEMP = 50 }
							check_variable = { JAP_popularity_of_party_var > JAP_popularity_of_party_var_TEMP }
							tooltip = JAP_popularity_of_party_var_check_tt
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				OR = { 
					AND = { 
						has_country_flag = NW_JAP_318_event_flag
						has_country_flag = NW_JAP_372_event_flag
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_318_event_flag }
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {

					ideology = socialism

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.717
	title = NW_JAP.717.t
	desc = { 
		text = NW_JAP.717.d.a
		trigger = { NOT = { GER = { has_government = fascism } } }
	}
	desc = { 
		text = NW_JAP.717.d.b
		trigger = { GER = { has_government = fascism } }
	}
	trigger = { 
		
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.717" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.717.a
		set_country_flag = JAP_plan_fugu_was_accepted
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = JAP_plan_fugu_category
		if = { 
			limit = { GER = { has_government = fascism } }
			GER = { 
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = JAP_plan_Fugu_active_op
					target = ROOT
				}
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = JAP_plan_Fugu_active_op
					target = ROOT
				} 
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				1031 = { is_controlled_by = JAP } 
				1145 = { is_controlled_by = JAP } 
			}
			country_event = NW_JAP.718
		}
		else = { 
			MAN = { country_event = NW_JAP.719 }
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.717.b
		# тут ивент про литовского посла нужен 
	}
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.717.c
		if = { 
			limit = { GER = { has_government = fascism } }
			GER = { 
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = JAP_plan_Fugu_was_rejected_op
					target = ROOT
				}
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = JAP_plan_Fugu_was_rejected_op
					target = ROOT
				} 
			}
		}
	}
}

# Раскрытие шпионской сети в Токио
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.721
	title = NW_JAP.721.t
	desc = NW_JAP.721.d
	trigger = { 
		date > 1941.10.01
		tag = JAP
		SOV = { has_civil_war = no }
		country_exists = SOV
		NOT = { 
			has_war_with = SOV 
			has_global_flag = THE_MOTHER_OF_ORDER_FLAG
			has_global_flag = WORLD_OF_SPLIT_FLAG
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.721" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.721.a
		trigger = { 
			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Fumimaro_Konoe ruling_only = yes } 
		}
		add_political_power = -30 
		set_country_flag = JAP_incident_with_zorge
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_government = fascism 
				#NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_478_flag } ну вроде эти три проверки не нужны из-за условий у Мацуоки
				#NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_477_flag } а зачем я тогда прописывал эти флаги в ивентах то
				#NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_467_flag } ёмоё
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = JAP_Yosuke_Matsuoka
					JAP_Yosuke_Matsuoka = {
						is_country_leader = no
						NOT = { has_character_flag = JAP_Yosuke_Matsuoka_sick }
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Yosuke_Matsuoka
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nationalism_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_former_President_of_Mantetsu JAP_master_of_a_Hundred_Thousand_Words }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_Matsuoka_Office } }
					complete_national_focus = JAP_Matsuoka_Office
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Seigo_Nakano
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = totalism
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_supporter_of_parliamentary_politics JAP_charismatic_agitator }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = { 
			if = {
				limit = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_Hiranuma_Kiichiro }
					promote_character = JAP_Hiranuma_Kiichiro
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Hiranuma_Kiichiro
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						desc = "POLITICS_HIRANUMA_KIICHIRO_DESC"
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_the_hidden_schemer JAP_a_representative_of_the_old_elites }
					}
				}
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party10 name = JAP_neutrality_party10 }
		}
		news_event = NW_JAP_news.87
	}
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.721.b
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Fumimaro_Konoe ruling_only = yes } }
		}
		add_political_power = -30 
		set_country_flag = JAP_incident_with_zorge
	}
}

	hidden = yes
    id = NW_JAP.724
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): hidden event NW_JAP.724" }
	immediate = {
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_government = neutrality 
				has_country_flag = JAP_cabinet_generic_system_active
			}
			set_country_flag = JAP_cabinet_expired_flag
		}
	}
} 

# Выборы в парламент [номер текущего года] года
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.725
	title = NW_JAP.725.t
	desc = NW_JAP.725.desc
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = JAP_cancel_elections 
			has_country_flag = JAP_skip_election_of_1940
			has_completed_focus = JAP_advisory_election_reform
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.725" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.725.a
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = JAP_shinshinto_was_created_flag 
			}
		}
		set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = JAP_democratic_party name = JAP_democratic_party }
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.015 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.015 }
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.725 days = 1460 }
			if = { 
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Keisuke_Okada ruling_only = yes } }
				set_country_flag = JAP_block_democracy 
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.725.b
		trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = JAP_shinshinto_was_created_flag 
		}
		set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = JAP_democratic_party4 name = JAP_democratic_party4 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.015 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.015 }
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.725 days = 1460 } 
			if = { 
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Keisuke_Okada ruling_only = yes } }
				set_country_flag = JAP_block_democracy 
			}
		}
	}
}

# Подготовка к выборам в парламент
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.726
	title = NW_JAP.726.t
	desc = NW_JAP.726.d
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = JAP_cancel_elections 
			has_country_flag = JAP_skip_election_of_1940
		}
		has_completed_focus = JAP_advisory_election_reform
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_NW_JAP.
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.726" }
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.726.a
		trigger = { 
			OR = { 
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = monarchy
				has_government = technocracy
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = add_aut_in_coalition
		if = { 
			limit = { has_government = fascism }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:monarchy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:technocracy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:democratic }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { has_government = monarchy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:fascism }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:technocracy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:democratic }
		}
		else = { 
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:fascism }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:monarchy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:democratic }
		}
		add_to_array = { coalition_array = token:neutrality }
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.727 days = 20 } 
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.726 days = 1460 } 
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.726.b
		trigger = { 
			OR = { 
				has_government = neutrality
				has_government = technocracy
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = add_fasc_in_coalition
		if = { 
			limit = { has_government = neutrality }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:monarchy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:technocracy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:democratic }
		}
		else = { 
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:neutrality }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:monarchy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:democratic }
		}
		add_to_array = { coalition_array = token:fascism }
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.727 days = 20 } 
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.726 days = 1460 } 
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.726.c
		trigger = { 
			has_government = neutrality
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = add_fasc_in_coalition
		remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:fascism }
		remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:technocracy }
		remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:democratic }
		add_to_array = { coalition_array = token:monarchy }
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.727 days = 20 } 
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.726 days = 1460 } 
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.726.d
		trigger = { 
			has_government = neutrality
			has_government = fascism
			has_government = monarchy
			has_government = technocracy
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { has_government = neutrality }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:monarchy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:technocracy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:fascism }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { has_government = fascism }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:neutrality }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:technocracy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:monarchy }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { has_government = monarchy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:fascism }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:technocracy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:neutrality }
		}
		else = { 
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:neutrality }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:monarchy }
			remove_from_array = { coalition_array = token:fascism }
		}
		add_to_array = { coalition_array = token:democratic }
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.727 days = 20 } 
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.726 days = 1460 } 
		}
	}
}

		set_country_flag = JAP_Shigeru_Yoshida_FA_minister
	}
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.746.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = JAP_Hachiro_Arita
		JAP_foreign_affairs_minister_clear_effect
		set_country_flag = JAP_Hachiro_Arita_FA_minister
	}
	option = { 
		name = NW_JAP.746.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = JAP_Tosio_Siratori
		JAP_foreign_affairs_minister_clear_effect
		set_country_flag = JAP_Tosio_Siratori_FA_minister
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = -5 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes	
		if = { 
			limit = { has_government = neutrality }
			add_stability = -0.05 
		}
	}
}

	id = NW_JAP_news.79

	desc = NW_JAP_news.79.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_NW_JAP_news.79
	major = yes
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { ENG = { has_war_with = major } }
		ENG = { has_civil_war = no }
		date > 1937.04.01
		date < 1937.05.01
		NOT = { 
			has_global_flag = THE_MOTHER_OF_ORDER_FLAG
			has_global_flag = WORLD_OF_SPLIT_FLAG
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_news.79.a
	}
}
